  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_bdc06c5f-1a11-47bd-ad9e-1b0a7ad31052'
      });

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    So the part where her rape was described was written from Pheobe's point of view and she always believed it was the friend because she had been with t<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    So the part where her rape was described was written from Pheobe's point of view and she always believed it was the friend because she had been with the friend that night. The pool shed was dark and pheobe couldn't see but Reed later tells her it was actually him and not his friend that followed her that night. <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>

And the sexy new boss is everything Dan despises—a meddling bimbo who doesn't know a pigskin from a pitcher's mound.</i></b>

  <span id="freeText15034011717224898242" style="display:none"><br><blockquote> <b><i>The Windy City isn't quite ready for Phoebe Somerville—the outrageous, curvaceous New York knockout who has just inherited the Chicago Stars football team. And Phoebe is definitely not ready for the Stars' head coach, former gridiron legend Dan Calebow, a sexist jock taskmaster with a one-track mind. Calebow is everything Phoebe abhors. And the sexy new boss is everything Dan despises—a meddling bimbo who doesn't know a pigskin from a pitcher's mound.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425634858i/13913125.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Dan is alpha, opinionated, chauvanistic, thick-skinned! I LOVED HIM.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425635413i/13913159._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>She was, without a doubt, the most worthless, spineless, silliest excuse for a human being he'd ever met in his life.</b>

It was as good if not better the second time 'round.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425634858i/13913126._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Phoebe was great. She'd been through a lot in her life and sort of came across as a brainless bimbo. But she was far from brainless and not at all like a bimbo. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"She sure doesn't know much about football. In the third quarter she cheered when we went offside."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>LOL, you and me both, Phoebe. Haven't a clue about American Football.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425634858i/13913127.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>What was his brainy bimbo up to now?</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ron was a great side-kick. He sure showed 'em!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425634858i/13913128.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The book is over 20 years old. Can you tell? Yes, but that doesn't take away from the enjoyment of the book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>It wasn't enough. He wanted more. More of her sex. Her heart. Her soul.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425634858i/13913129._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I liked Molly too. Great that she gets her own story in another book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425634858i/13913130.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I'm glad my friends are discovering these books!<br><br></span>

<div id="review_1602893728" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1602893728" />
    <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell"><img alt="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584062476p2/2190064.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1602893728?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell">Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780061555817" href="/book/show/5198673-it-had-to-be-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=kissing-books">kissing-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=sports-romance">sports-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1602893728" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12337630219528270354"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> || <a href='https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> || <a href='https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> || <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> || <a href='https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest</a><br/><br/><br/>Phoebe Summerville is like a cross between Elle Woods and Peg Bundy - she's rich, she's tacky, everyone writes her off as a dumb bimbo. However, she's quite a bit more clever and complicated than anyone gives her credit for, including her father, who disliked her so much that he decided to screw with her from beyond the grave: instead of being disinherited as per his original plan, he's giving her his football team, the Chicago Stars, fo</span>
  <span id="freeText12337630219528270354" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>Phoebe Summerville is like a cross between Elle Woods and Peg Bundy - she's rich, she's tacky, everyone writes her off as a dumb bimbo. However, she's quite a bit more clever and complicated than anyone gives her credit for, including her father, who disliked her so much that he decided to screw with her from beyond the grave: instead of being disinherited as per his original plan, he's giving her his football team, the Chicago Stars, for a year. If the team loses the NFL playoffs, she gets $100,000 and ownership reverts to her icky cousin, Reed. If she wins, she keeps the team. Damned if she does, damned if she doesn't.<br><br><br><br>Dan Calebow, the coach of the Stars, is highly displeased when he finds out who the new owner is. He's even more displeased when he finds himself inexplicably attracted to her. I know the Goodreads blurb describes him as "a sexist jock taskmaster with a one-track mind", but this doesn't even come close to describing what a piece of work this man is, and what he does to Phoebe.<br><br><br><br>First, let me say that I loved the premise behind this book. I love books that show that women can be fashionable, girly, ditzy, <i>and </i>smart. Legally Blonde and Clueless are two of my favorite movies, and for a while I thought this book was going to be like that, with Phoebe learning more about management and football while also teaching the players "the bend and snap." Because Phoebe was a great character, and her tacky, over-the-top 90s outfits are all kinds of awesome.<br><br><br><br>My problem with the book is Dan. Just Dan. And while it seems a bit harsh, I know, to lower the ratings of a book so dramatically just because one of the characters ticked me off, Dan is the love interest and one of the narrators, so he's kind of inescapable. In the first scene from his POV, we're led to believe that he's having sex with a sixteen-year-old high school cheerleader. In actuality, it's his ex-wife, Valerie, who likes to play kinky roleplaying games, but I felt like I was led on way too long into thinking that this hero is actually the type of man to sleep with underage women.<br><br><br><br>Minus one.<br><br><br><br>Dan is also kind of creepy. Even as he's having kinky sex with his ex-wife, he's shopping for the next one, and eventually hones in on a preschool teacher named Sharon Anderson. So he's dating this girl while having sex with his ex-wife and having sexual thoughts about Phoebe. The worst part is, Sharon never finds out about any of this. Dan breaks up with her eventually, and tells her it's because she wasn't what he was looking for after all, and that's the end of it. Poor Sharon never finds out.<br><br><br><br>Minus two.<br><br><br><br>At one point, Dan and his ex-wife are planning rape play. When Phoebe drops by unexpectedly, Dan mistakes her for his ex-wife and drags her off into the woods while saying all these threatening things. Phoebe, who is a rape victim, freaks out, and Dan doesn't realize anything is wrong until she starts screaming. His excuse is that it's dark. And he doesn't really feel as sorry as he should have.<br><br><br><br>Minus three.<br><br><br><br>Towards the end of the book, Dan tells Phoebe that he doesn't feel comfortable dating someone with the power to fire him.<br><br><br><br>Minus four.<br><br><br><br>Also, the inclusion of this line:<br><br><i>What good were curvy hips and full breasts if she couldn't let a man caress them, if they would never bring a baby into the world or nuture its new life?</i> (142)<br><br><br><br>Minus five.<br><br><br><br>And the inclusion of this line:<br><br><i>Phoebe was a curvy, buxom , good-time girl, custom-designed by God for just this kind of romp </i>(239)<i>.</i><br><br><br><br>Minus six.<i> </i><br><br><br><br>Plus, there were some weird stylistic choices in the narrative style that just felt odd to me. For example:<br><br><br><br><i>Her curved hips swayed in a sassy walk that seemed to have a language all its own</i><br><br><br><br><i>Hot cha cha<br>Hot cha cha<br>Hot hot<br>Cha cha cha cha</i> (55).<br><br><br><br>I have no idea if this is a reference to something or what it's supposed to mean, but the author seems to like it, because she repeats it several times. She has a couple favorite words that are also repeated several times, like "peek-a-boo", "sassy", and "delirious."<br><br><br><br>This line was kind of weird as well.<br><br><br><br><i>Like plantation slaves, the National Football League's Chicago Stars had come to pay homage to the man who owned them</i> (5).<br><br><br><br>In addition to Dan, I also despised Molly, Phoebe's younger half-sister. She's such a sh*t to her sister, despite everything Phoebe does for her. Molly's not happy at school? Phoebe changes schools for her. Molly's not happy at home? She gets to live with Phoebe. Molly feels drab? Phoebe offers to go clothes shopping with her. How does Molly repay her? By putting her down and making her feel bad about herself every chance she gets, and at one point, telling a stranger (Dan) that Phoebe hits her.<br><br><br><br>How does Dan react to this? In the end, he pretty much laughs it off. It becomes a joke at the end.<br><br><br><br>I <b>loved </b>Phoebe's character and I liked how she talked about what good people her horrible father's wives were. She never slut-shames any of her stepmothers and at one point says that they're strong women because they were survivors who did the best they could to live their lives. I also loved her interactions with the players and with Ron, and her locker room speech was really cute. I also liked how when she found out about Dan going out with Sharon, she didn't blame Sharon. She blamed Dan. Isn't that refreshing? Blaming the cheater instead of the <i>cheatee</i>? I thought so.<br><br><br><br>Phoebe was clever and a schemer, and she wasn't afraid to live her life. Even though she was raped, and suffered blow after blow to her self-esteem, she learned to take advantage of the male gaze, and how to cow male bullies by beating them at their own game. She was a wonderful, complicated, quirky heroine, and it made me so sad to see her paired off with such a terrible, terrible hero.<br><br><br><br>The dated 90s references were so amusing. Rows of payphones in a locker room? Chokers? LOL.<br><br><br><br>P.S. Donald Trump makes a random paragraph-long cameo.<br><br><br><br>2 to 2.5 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12337630219528270354" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer822671902" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16897049505447485084">***4.5 <b>NOW</b> stars***<br/><br/><b>You’re my only failure. My only failure, Phoebe.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389663763i/8046764._SX540_.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b><br/>Perfect book for getting in the spirit of the upcoming Super Bowl XLVIII (2/2/2014).</b><br/><br/><b>Phoebe</b> is a sexy underestimated daughter of a football owner (Chicago Stars). When her father sudden dies she inherits his team. Unfortunately, her father’s “gift” wasn’t given out of kindness. Her father had always seen her as a failure and this opportunity to run the team was a test. She must win the championship or she will lose any inheritance</span>
  <span id="freeText16897049505447485084" style="display:none">***4.5 <b>NOW</b> stars***<br><br><b>You’re my only failure. My only failure, Phoebe.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389663763i/8046764._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><br>Perfect book for getting in the spirit of the upcoming Super Bowl XLVIII (2/2/2014).</b><br><br><b>Phoebe</b> is a sexy underestimated daughter of a football owner (Chicago Stars). When her father sudden dies she inherits his team. Unfortunately, her father’s “gift” wasn’t given out of kindness. Her father had always seen her as a failure and this opportunity to run the team was a test. She must win the championship or she will lose any inheritance.<br><br><b>Dan</b> is the cocky coach of the Chicago Stars. He has little faith in the new owner of the team. Butting heads and misunderstandings overshadow their relationship. The chemistry between these two is best summarized by them: <blockquote>
<b><i>”I guess we’re like oil and water.” </i></b> -Phoebe<br><b><i>”I’d say we’re more like gasoline and a blowtorch.” </i></b> -Dan</blockquote><br><b>It Had To Be You</b> just celebrated its 20th year in publication. It has some cheesy moments but that seems to be common with books written in the 90's. This was my first book by Susan Elizabeth Phillips and it won’t be my last. <br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73070.It_Had_to_Be_You__Chicago_Stars___1_" title="It Had to Be You (Chicago Stars, #1) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73095.Dream_a_Little_Dream__Chicago_Stars___4_" title="Dream a Little Dream (Chicago Stars, #4) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/118126465?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Heather " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Heather " href="/user/show/2736715-lady-heather">Lady Heather </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6651365-it-had-to-be-you">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">contemporary romance, domineering alpha males &amp; broken women trying to find their HEA</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=1st-in-a-series">1st-in-a-series</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer118126465" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12970931977362313115"><br/>WOW! <br/><br/>What an amazing read, and although I don't often read sports-romance books (especially football..hey I'm Canadian if anything, I'd read a romance with hockey..Eh?..LOL) this was really good!<br/><br/>This happened <i> a lot </i> while reading this story<br/><br/><a href='http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%206/youknowyouhaveagoodbookwhen.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380338716i/695683.jpg' alt=' photo youknowyouhaveagoodbookwhen.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>I really, really, really liked Dan. I loved his complexity, strength, loyalty, gentleness, and his own desire for a HEA.<br/>He is not what I'm used to in a 'hero', but he was written beautifully! He just seemed SO real, with many layers.<br/>I was wonderful to rea</span>
  <span id="freeText12970931977362313115" style="display:none"><br>WOW! <br><br>What an amazing read, and although I don't often read sports-romance books (especially football..hey I'm Canadian if anything, I'd read a romance with hockey..Eh?..LOL) this was really good!<br><br>This happened <i> a lot </i> while reading this story<br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%206/youknowyouhaveagoodbookwhen.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380338716i/695683.jpg" alt=" photo youknowyouhaveagoodbookwhen.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I really, really, really liked Dan. I loved his complexity, strength, loyalty, gentleness, and his own desire for a HEA.<br>He is not what I'm used to in a 'hero', but he was written beautifully! He just seemed SO real, with many layers.<br>I was wonderful to read how frustrated, and angry Dan would get when trying to talk to, or even relate to Phoebe<br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%206/whyisitsohardtotalktoyou-1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380338716ra/695684.gif" alt=" photo whyisitsohardtotalktoyou-1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>.. and Phoebe, you were AMAZING! Your upbringing and what happened to you broke my heart, but GIRRRL.. YOU. ARE. A. SURVIVOR! You did what you had to do in order to survive and what <i>amazed</i> me about your character was that you did not become cold and bitter, but if anything you were insecure (but never let it show), and yet still so strong and able to adapt to any and all situations brilliantly! <br><br>All you ever wanted was to be accepted and loved.<br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%206/moregoodthanbad.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380338716ra/695685.gif" alt=" photo moregoodthanbad.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>LOVED THIS STORY! <br><br>Definitely one of my favorites! <br></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6408039881982336364"><b>5 STARS</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects%203/tumblr_nej70pGreD1t5d99go1_500.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965643._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo tumblr_nej70pGreD1t5d99go1_500.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>What can I say? Another 5 star book? Most definitely!!! I’m starting to think Susan Elizabeth Phillips cannot write a bad book… either that or she has most definitely found the key to my heart. These books exemplify the delicate balance of intense emotion, witty dialogue and comic relief. I have nothing but high praise and giddy admiration for this author and her fabulous books. <br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women%202/tumblr_ln7neiSUNx1qg6c3ko1_500.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965644._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo tumblr_ln7neiSUNx1qg6c3ko1_500.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Phoebe Sommerville</b> was a thirty-three year old outrageous Manhattan socialite</span>
  <span id="freeText6408039881982336364" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects%203/tumblr_nej70pGreD1t5d99go1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965643._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_nej70pGreD1t5d99go1_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What can I say? Another 5 star book? Most definitely!!! I’m starting to think Susan Elizabeth Phillips cannot write a bad book… either that or she has most definitely found the key to my heart. These books exemplify the delicate balance of intense emotion, witty dialogue and comic relief. I have nothing but high praise and giddy admiration for this author and her fabulous books. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women%202/tumblr_ln7neiSUNx1qg6c3ko1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965644._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_ln7neiSUNx1qg6c3ko1_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Phoebe Sommerville</b> was a thirty-three year old outrageous Manhattan socialite, who was the notorious mistress of a famous Spanish painter. Returning to Chicago for her father’s funeral, Phoebe, who had believed herself disinherited from her father’s will, is shocked to find that he has left her the sole owner of his Chicago Stars NFL football team. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects%203/il_570xN.320037547.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965647._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo il_570xN.320037547.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Phoebe, who not only has no knowledge of football, also has no interest in accepting this very public responsibility. As well.. the organization has no intension of having this buxom bimbo take over their organization. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men2/090214tombrady_1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965645._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 090214tombrady_1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Dan Calabow</b> is a retired star quarterback, who is now the head coach of the <b>Chicago Stars</b> football team. He is sexist, he is hot-headed, and he is determined to rescue his team from this useless airhead, who is not only an embarrassment to his organization but who is also his boss. But his biggest problem… is that he seems to be obsessed with her. And boy does he have a funny way of showing it! <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Gifs2/yP38geM.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426035769ra/13965882.gif" alt=" photo yP38geM.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“I must have your promise, Coach, that you won't hurt her."<br>"I promise."<br>"You spoke a bit too quickly for my taste. I don't quite believe you."<br>"I'm a man of my word, and I promise that I won't hurt her. When I murder her, I'll do it real quick, so she won't feel a thing."<br>Viktor sighed. "That's exactly what I was afraid of.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/5e828fc06873074d7c2eabf0a4ab5cda.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965649.jpg" alt=" photo 5e828fc06873074d7c2eabf0a4ab5cda.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>”I can’t tolerate the idea of anyone feeling sorry for me.”  “You’d rather have everyone dislike you?” <br>She forced a cocky smile as she reached for the knob. “I’m comfortable with contempt. It’s pity I can’t stand.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Couples/tumblr_nkcxsuecqC1qak0uxo1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965651._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_nkcxsuecqC1qak0uxo1_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>”I guess we’re oil and water.”<br> “I’d say we’re more like gasoline and a blowtorch.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects%203/200c42c24d6fd09d9b966ec661ad6a16.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965650._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 200c42c24d6fd09d9b966ec661ad6a16.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>”The photographs are beautiful, Phoebe. Both of us know that. But they’re still not as pretty as you are.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men2/B8ztU0ICIAAO_jd.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426034737i/13965648.png" alt=" photo B8ztU0ICIAAO_jd.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>”I, Mr. Pigskin-For-Brains, am the owner of this football team; not you. Do I make myself absolutely clear?”</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects%203/tumblr_lg3na34OF51qa1ix6o1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>
  <i>”We’re heading straight for the bedroom, darlin’. Since there’s a good chance I’m going to have a heart attack before the night’s over, I want to die in my own bed.”</i>
</b><br><br>This is a fantastically funny and endearing love story. It is an explosion of bad tempers and sexual attraction, past traumas and abandoned dreams. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Animals/44488D29-3A15-4916-83BB-D83CC1717B01.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_86438584" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/86438584" />
    <a title="valee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2320890-valee"><img alt="valee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1443365004p2/2320890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/86438584?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="valee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="valee" href="/user/show/2320890-valee">valee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2320890-valee?shelf=cont-romance">cont-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer86438584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11777320590960861670">I just have no words to describe how much I loved this book. It was amazing! Maybe I was just in the right mood for this kind of read or maybe it really is a terrific read. I just know that apart from LK's Travises series, I had never, ever enjoyed a contemporary romance as much as I did this one and the Travises. And yes, it was that good for me. Well maybe not that good, lol, but definitely the closest I will ever find.<br/><br/>I loved Phoebe! She was an amazing heroine. Everything about her was so app</span>
  <span id="freeText11777320590960861670" style="display:none">I just have no words to describe how much I loved this book. It was amazing! Maybe I was just in the right mood for this kind of read or maybe it really is a terrific read. I just know that apart from LK's Travises series, I had never, ever enjoyed a contemporary romance as much as I did this one and the Travises. And yes, it was that good for me. Well maybe not that good, lol, but definitely the closest I will ever find.<br /><br />I loved Phoebe! She was an amazing heroine. Everything about her was so appealing. She was just so broken and lost, and so many things were wrong with her at the beginning. But we get to see her grow into the kind of person we all wanna be. She still was very funny at the beginning, lol, so many scenes made me laugh so hard I had to stop reading the book and analyze them over and over again. Oh Pooh (He's the dog for those who have not read it yet), you were my favorite character, so sweet. Phoebe was so strong and she definitely deserved her HEA! <br /><br />Now let's get to the good stuff! Yes Dan Calebow, I'm talking about you. What a hero. You know, maybe it's just me that I have been reading paranormal for too long and heroes were always the same. Dan was so different from every other hero I have read about so far. He felt so real, I hated him at the beginning, and ended LOVING him, yes LOVING him. How could I not? He was so human, so real and had his personal demons to confront as Phoebe did. <br /><br />Of course they made it work out at the end together, it's romance after all, lol, but the story makes you need to keep reading until you finish the it. There's so many emotions enclosed in this book. I wanted to laugh sometimes and cry others, even both at the same time. I was frustrated and extremely exhilarated the next second. That's how good the book is. <br /><br />I don't know why so many did not gave more than 3 stars to this book. IMHO this was a terrific contemporary romance and I loved every second of it. I'm dying to read more in this amazing series. As always Ally you were right. Here goes another book into my favs list! Enjoy people, definitely a must read for romance lovers.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11777320590960861670" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=over-25">over-25</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=enemy-to-lover">enemy-to-lover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1290305671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17420606491883328828"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1585150380i/29167821._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My first by SEP and I loved it. The book was written 25 years ago and it is a traditional contemporary romance of enemies to lovers troupe. Even though it was written a long time ago, I loved being taken back to 1994. As I’m in my 50’s, I remembered so many references and loved being brought back in time.<br/><br/>Phoebe Summerville is the new owner of the Chicago Stars football team. It was left to her by her deceased estranged father. She plays the part of a blonde bimbo but she is anything but that. Sh</span>
  <span id="freeText17420606491883328828" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1585150380i/29167821._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My first by SEP and I loved it. The book was written 25 years ago and it is a traditional contemporary romance of enemies to lovers troupe. Even though it was written a long time ago, I loved being taken back to 1994. As I’m in my 50’s, I remembered so many references and loved being brought back in time.<br><br>Phoebe Summerville is the new owner of the Chicago Stars football team. It was left to her by her deceased estranged father. She plays the part of a blonde bimbo but she is anything but that. She is beautiful, sexy, flirtatious, and smart and I adored her. <br><br>Dan Calebow, is the quintessential football player turned coach. He’s cocky, arrogant, handsome, hot headed, and sexist. But hey, once you meet him, you can’t help but fall in love with his caveman antics.<br><br>These two are oil and water. They don’t mix but when they do it’s sassy, feisty, fabulous and very combustible. Being on the sideline while they navigate their feelings is awesome, just like a perfectly executed touchdown pass!!!<br><br>I will say that I also loved all the secondary characters....Molly, Ron, and Bobby Tom were perfect!! I would definitely recommend this oldie (1994) but goodie romance!!</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9829949293215453919">Absolutely fantastic read!!!<br/><br/>In fact, i might say, the best I ve read this year (and the book was first published almost over 20 years ago *facepalm* so, in my eyes, the words "it 's never too late" and "never say never" have a whole new meaning...) considering the genre.<br/><br/>This book can't be presented through out the re-telling of the storyline, cause that would be impossible to do without spilling it all and spoiling it...so, I m gonna stick to the old folks' saying: "less is more" 😉<br/><br/>But to appease</span>
  <span id="freeText9829949293215453919" style="display:none">Absolutely fantastic read!!!<br /><br />In fact, i might say, the best I ve read this year (and the book was first published almost over 20 years ago *facepalm* so, in my eyes, the words "it 's never too late" and "never say never" have a whole new meaning...) considering the genre.<br /><br />This book can't be presented through out the re-telling of the storyline, cause that would be impossible to do without spilling it all and spoiling it...so, I m gonna stick to the old folks' saying: "less is more" 😉<br /><br />But to appease my own soul cause of the need to express my admiration and thrill i had during and after the reading, I will add this: <b>
  <i>you might think according to the blurb that this is another case of a <u>light rom/com sport drama à la Jerry McGuire</u> and in some aspects, yeah, I guess it is...but it's also so much more...<br /><br />Incredible, effortless writing pulls you in from page one into the world of <b>sport drama and intrigue with multiple layered characters that feel so palpably raw and real as you watch them interact, feel, express their thoughts and emotions...</b><br /><br />Then you are enveloped into this thrill of <b>action sequences, emotional rollercoaster with a touch of suspense and twist</b> that you suddenly realize you've been holding your breath for quite a while and the relief from exhaling is substantialy close to a complete catharsis<br /><br />Highly recommended!</i>
</b><br /><br />And once again, thanks <b>Anna's Ramblings</b> for pointing out this author to me!</span>

<div id="review_121022680" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/121022680" />
    <a title="Jane Stewart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3789528-jane-stewart"><img alt="Jane Stewart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346001994p2/3789528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/121022680?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jane Stewart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jane Stewart" href="/user/show/3789528-jane-stewart">Jane Stewart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=5-star-romance">5-star-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=contemporary-sports-romance">contemporary-sports-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=humorous-contemporary-romance">humorous-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=football">football</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer121022680" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8616620600962921439">It was so fun to be in this book.<br/><br/>I’ve read the paperback three times and recently listened to the audiobook. I laughed a lot the first time I read it. I didn’t laugh as much in subsequent reads because I knew what to expect, but I still loved it.<br/><br/>Phoebe’s mother died early and her father didn’t love her. He kept her away in boarding schools and camps. She was raped, but her father didn’t believe her. She creates a false front, looking and acting like a Marilyn Monroe-Mae West-blond-bombshell-bimb</span>
  <span id="freeText8616620600962921439" style="display:none">It was so fun to be in this book.<br /><br />I’ve read the paperback three times and recently listened to the audiobook. I laughed a lot the first time I read it. I didn’t laugh as much in subsequent reads because I knew what to expect, but I still loved it.<br /><br />Phoebe’s mother died early and her father didn’t love her. He kept her away in boarding schools and camps. She was raped, but her father didn’t believe her. She creates a false front, looking and acting like a Marilyn Monroe-Mae West-blond-bombshell-bimbo. She’s afraid of sex, but she talks as if she has many lovers. She appears silly and not smart, but underneath she is very smart. Because of this false front her dialogue does not fit her inner motivations. But it’s believable because her false front is her protection. And it provides good dialogue and conflict.<br /><br />There are no details about the rape. It consists of Phoebe telling her father afterwards that she has been raped. Some readers avoid books with rape scenes. I think this might be mild enough not to bother them.<br /><br />Dan was a football star and is now head coach of a pro football team. Dan and Phoebe conflicts are entertaining. And Dan’s intense desire for Phoebe melts me. There’s some really cool passion.<br /><br />SEMI-SPOILER ABOUT DAN’S MOTIVATIONS:<br />Dan’s had sex with lots of women, but he no longer wants that. He’s looking for a wife who likes domestic activities and children. He starts dating a kindergarten teacher thinking she fits. But then he finds himself drawn to Phoebe. He can’t resist his lust for her. Yet he tries to resist as the honorable thing to do since he doesn’t view Phoebe as marriage material.<br />END SPOILER.<br /><br />AUDIOBOOK NARRATOR:<br />Anna Fields did a great job with male and female voices.<br /><br />DATA:<br />Narrative mode: 3rd person. Story length: 387 pages. Swearing language: strong, including religious swear words. Sexual language: none. Number of sex or kissing scenes: about 8. Setting: current day mostly Chicago, Illinois area. Copyright: 1994. Genre: contemporary sports romance, football.<br /><br />OTHER BOOKS:<br />To date, I’ve read all books by Susan Elizabeth Phillips, except for the first one which is out of print. Dates below are copyright dates. In the two series, I recommend reading them in order (but not required). Some characters have minor parts flowing into future books. It’s nice knowing their backgrounds.<br /><br />WYNETTE, TEXAS:<br />5 stars. Glitter Baby 1987 &amp; 2009 (2009 version has changes)<br />4 ½ stars. Fancy Pants 1989<br />5 stars. <div id="review_1297621884" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1297621884" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1297621884?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog">Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18524013-it-had-to-be-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-fav-series">book-1-of-fav-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=jock-straps-r-us">jock-straps-r-us</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=just-one-more-try">just-one-more-try</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=library-loan">library-loan</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1297621884" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5384259439738650814">I owe a huge debt of gratitude to my friends Karen, Mo and Sharon for clogging my feed with updates of binge reading books by Susan Elizabeth Phillips. Because of them I just may have found a new favorite author. I definitely discovered a delightful sports romance to add to my favorites bookshelf.<br/><br/><i>It Had to Be You</i> is old-school romance at its finest and I’m not talking about the fact that it was written over 20 years ago. In fact, if it weren’t for some dated references (cassette tapes, VCR, a Wa</span>
  <span id="freeText5384259439738650814" style="display:none">I owe a huge debt of gratitude to my friends Karen, Mo and Sharon for clogging my feed with updates of binge reading books by Susan Elizabeth Phillips. Because of them I just may have found a new favorite author. I definitely discovered a delightful sports romance to add to my favorites bookshelf.<br><br><i>It Had to Be You</i> is old-school romance at its finest and I’m not talking about the fact that it was written over 20 years ago. In fact, if it weren’t for some dated references (cassette tapes, VCR, a Walkman, OJ Simpson as the sportscaster, etc.) it could very well have been a new release. But the refreshing writing style sets this book apart from its more modern counterparts and makes it reminiscent of the types of romance novels that made me fall in love with the genre. This book has the perfect blend of poignancy and humor.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Poor Phoebe. When are you going to finish inventing yourself?”<br>“When I get it right,” she said softly.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I guess we’re oil and water.”<br>“I’d say we’re more like gasoline and blowtorch.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>I loved the slow burn of not just the romance between Phoebe and Dan but the relationship between Phoebe and her sister and the bromance between Ron and Dan as well. The love scenes are sexy and pack a lot of heat without feeling raunchy. <br><br>Susan Elizabeth Phillips has created a wonderful cast of characters, including the lovable members of the Chicago Stars football team. My favorite character, however, is Phoebe. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436450772i/15460663.jpg" alt=" photo Phoebe1_zpsrlv1dg9s.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She’s such a complex character: curvaceous, flamboyant, airheaded sexpot, wounded survivor, witty, smart. She is so much more than she appears to be on the outside.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Sometimes I think bimbo is just another word men made up so they could feel superior to women who are better at survival than they are.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>It was a joy seeing the way Susan Elizabeth Phillips constructed her evolution.<br><br>I’m looking forward to reading the other books in the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5384259439738650814" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15407163192034663354">If i want to speak about the books that can kill me with their Romance and breathtaking moments I'm going to put this book on top of my list. I loved the combination of sports and romance in this book, it was totally amazing and truned it so attractive that grab your attention until the end and take your breath away. I couldn't stop reading it and I enjoyed it so much.<br/>the characters, romance, plot and everything was so good!! I really missed reading this type of books. Actually I prefer fantasy </span>
  <span id="freeText15407163192034663354" style="display:none">If i want to speak about the books that can kill me with their Romance and breathtaking moments I'm going to put this book on top of my list. I loved the combination of sports and romance in this book, it was totally amazing and truned it so attractive that grab your attention until the end and take your breath away. I couldn't stop reading it and I enjoyed it so much.<br />the characters, romance, plot and everything was so good!! I really missed reading this type of books. Actually I prefer fantasy books more but reading this was such a great and fun experience. <br /><br />*** ( sorry if my reviews are not good enough, I try hard to do it better and I really work on it. Thanks for everything guys! 🙈) ****</span>

<div id="review_230961716" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/230961716" />
    <a title="Ronyell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell"><img alt="Ronyell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1506581787p2/1169488.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/230961716?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ronyell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ronyell" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell">Ronyell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=sexy-bad-boy-hero">sexy-bad-boy-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=manners">manners</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=aar-top-100-romance-books-2010">aar-top-100-romance-books-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=adult-book">adult-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=ronyell-s-epinions-reviews">ronyell-s-epinions-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=my-blog-reviews">my-blog-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=sports-related-books">sports-related-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=susan-elizabeth-philliips">susan-elizabeth-philliips</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer230961716" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3558553885387610864">To be honest, I have always been a huge fan of historical romance since it takes me to a time that is so completely different from the current times. However, after reading this little gem of a romance novel, I started to gain interest in the world of contemporary romance. “It Had To Be You” was the first romance novel I have read from author Susan Elizabeth Phillips and after I had read this book, I am definitely looking forward to reading more of her wonderful books! “It Had To Be You” is full</span>
  <span id="freeText3558553885387610864" style="display:none">To be honest, I have always been a huge fan of historical romance since it takes me to a time that is so completely different from the current times. However, after reading this little gem of a romance novel, I started to gain interest in the world of contemporary romance. “It Had To Be You” was the first romance novel I have read from author Susan Elizabeth Phillips and after I had read this book, I am definitely looking forward to reading more of her wonderful books! “It Had To Be You” is full of hot, sizzling romance, pure football fun and drama that will set any romance fans’ heads spinning!<br /><br />When Bert Somerville, the owner of the prized football team, the Chicago Stars, dies he left in his will that his estranged daughter, Phoebe Somerville, will inherit the football team after his death. Unfortunately, since Phoebe and her father never got along, there is a condition that Phoebe must follow in order to be successful in inheriting the football team. If the Chicago Stars are able to make it to the AFC Championships, then Phoebe will be able to inherit the football team and earn one thousand dollars, but if the team fails to win, then Phoebe’s cruel cousin, Reed Chandler, will inherit the football team. Things get more complicated when Phoebe meets the head football coach, Dan Calebow and at first sight, the two of them never got along. However, Phoebe and Dan will soon discover how true love can work in mysterious ways…especially on the football field!<br /><br />Alright, so now that you saw the cover of this book (a blown up photo of a woman’s chest) you are probably thinking that this book would turn out to be too kinky for anyone’s taste in romance novels. NO, that is not so! Susan Elizabeth Phillips has not only written a romance novel full of hot and sizzling love scenes, but she wrote a romance novel that is full of drama and love! Susan Elizabeth Phillips made the characters come to life in this novel, especially Phoebe Somerville and Dan Calebow! Let me just say that I just love Phoebe Somerville to death! Not only is Phoebe truly attractive to the boys, but she is extremely independent and I loved the way that she handles the football team with so much confidence, despite the fact that she does not know anything about football. I also loved the fact that Phoebe is always so determined to do everything right, no matter how hard the task is and I loved her relationship with her younger half-sister Molly and her attempts to make Molly see her as a good person, which truly makes Phoebe into such a caring heroine. It was also heartbreaking in hearing about Phoebe’s childhood and how she was raped at such a young age. I truly felt for her character when she experienced that horrible event and it was understandable why she would not let Dan near her in the first place. Now onto the good part and that’s the all handsome and all muscle hero, Dan Calebow! Dan Calebow is clearly one of my favorite romance heroes of all time because even though he has a terrible temper, he can be so caring and funny towards Phoebe and his dedication to football is truly inspiring in his nature. Also, his dream of marrying a woman who loves children and wants to start a family with him, is just so sweet and dreamy! I just love men who are so caring about having a family of their own to take care of! And do not forget the love scenes between Phoebe and Dan! They are truly smoking and romance fans everywhere will definitely be fanning themselves once they read through these love scenes between Dan and Phoebe!<br /><br />For those of you who do not like strong language and strong sex scenes, this novel has a lot of strong language and the sex scenes might be too explicit, so it would be best to skip over these scenes if it becomes too problematic.<br /><br />Overall, “It Had To Be You” is easily one of the best contemporary romances ever written and anyone who is interested in reading romance novels that deal with the love of sports has got to check this novel out!<br /><br /><b>Review is also on: <a href="http://rabbitearsbookblog.blogspot.com/2013/04/it-had-to-be-you-by-susan-elizabeth.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabbit Ears Book Blog</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3558553885387610864" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer169959219" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14319783343069263308"><br/><b>4 Stars! What started out as a book I thought I wasn't going to be too fond of, turned into a story I loved!</b><br/><br/>I read this entire series out of order. I started with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73080.Nobody_s_Baby_But_Mine__Chicago_Stars___3_' title='Nobody's Baby But Mine (Chicago Stars, #3) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips' rel='nofollow noopener'>Nobody's Baby But Mine</a>, which was good, then <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73095.Dream_a_Little_Dream__Chicago_Stars___4_' title='Dream a Little Dream (Chicago Stars, #4) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dream a Little Dream</a>, which was excellent and my favorite in the series. Then it was on to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73084.Heaven__Texas__Chicago_Stars___2_' title='Heaven, Texas (Chicago Stars, #2) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips' rel='nofollow noopener'>Heaven, Texas</a>, very good and funny, and now back to book one. So unlike me to do this, but hey, what can I say. Anyhoo, in those books you always hear about Phoebe and Dan Calebow, the owners of the St</span>
  <span id="freeText14319783343069263308" style="display:none"><br /><b>4 Stars! What started out as a book I thought I wasn't going to be too fond of, turned into a story I loved!</b><br /><br />I read this entire series out of order. I started with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73080.Nobody_s_Baby_But_Mine__Chicago_Stars___3_" title="Nobody's Baby But Mine (Chicago Stars, #3) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">Nobody's Baby But Mine</a>, which was good, then <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73095.Dream_a_Little_Dream__Chicago_Stars___4_" title="Dream a Little Dream (Chicago Stars, #4) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">Dream a Little Dream</a>, which was excellent and my favorite in the series. Then it was on to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73084.Heaven__Texas__Chicago_Stars___2_" title="Heaven, Texas (Chicago Stars, #2) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">Heaven, Texas</a>, very good and funny, and now back to book one. So unlike me to do this, but hey, what can I say. Anyhoo, in those books you always hear about Phoebe and Dan Calebow, the owners of the Stars, so I had to read their story for myself. Well, I was cringing a little in the beginning, particularly because of one scene, but this is SEP so I knew what I was reading was not <b>
  <i>really</i>
</b> what I was reading. It happened again a little later in the book, and of course my mind did the same thing, but once it was all explained, I breathed a sigh of relief and the story took hold. SEP worked her magic on me and I ended up loving Dan and Phoebe's story and seeing them both live their dream. The epilogue was beautiful!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6167303823345437414"><b>5 Throwback Stars<br/><br/><i>"Sometimes I think bimbo is just another word men made up so they could feel superior to women who are better at survival than they are.”</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520044214ra/25152602.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Many moons ago, as a freshman home from college, I discovered my mom’s collection of Susan Elizabeth Phillips books and I’ve never looked back. <i>It had to be you</i> was my very first SEP read and I’m so grateful I picked it up.<br/><br/>Originally, I gave this one a 4 star, but after my weekend reread I’m bumping it up to a 5. Yes, some of the references are</span>
  <span id="freeText6167303823345437414" style="display:none"><b>5 Throwback Stars<br><br><i>"Sometimes I think bimbo is just another word men made up so they could feel superior to women who are better at survival than they are.”</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520044214ra/25152602.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Many moons ago, as a freshman home from college, I discovered my mom’s collection of Susan Elizabeth Phillips books and I’ve never looked back. <i>It had to be you</i> was my very first SEP read and I’m so grateful I picked it up.<br><br>Originally, I gave this one a 4 star, but after my weekend reread I’m bumping it up to a 5. Yes, some of the references are dated (OJ Simpson still had a sportscaster job, y’all!) and it’s been a while since I’ve worn a pair of pleated shorts, but the story itself is still a winner. I laughed, I cried, I marveled at SEP’s ability to keep me interested in more than one storyline at a time. This book introduced this author to me and for that, I’ll forever be thankful. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6167303823345437414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780061793530" href="/book/show/10165225-it-had-to-be-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17575003-mich?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17575003-mich?shelf=good-new-to-me-author">good-new-to-me-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17575003-mich?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17575003-mich?shelf=cute-sweet">cute-sweet</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1654847129" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8199750501265165684"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "I disgraced MYSELF? Unless my memory’s faulty, you were the one who got evicted."<br/><br/>"I got ejected, not evicted. That was a football game, not a damn landlords’ convention." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Haha :) <br/><br/>I LOVE football, but I rarely read books about it for some reason. And it’s a weird thing to bother me, but I really don’t like it when there’s fake team names. Chicago <i>Stars</i>? Ugh, so fake. It puts me in the mindset of, <i>Ugh, this makes everything feel so fake.</i> I dunno. I’m weird.<br/><br/>Anyway, this book and I had</span>
  <span id="freeText8199750501265165684" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "I disgraced MYSELF? Unless my memory’s faulty, you were the one who got evicted."<br /><br />"I got ejected, not evicted. That was a football game, not a damn landlords’ convention." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Haha :) <br /><br />I LOVE football, but I rarely read books about it for some reason. And it’s a weird thing to bother me, but I really don’t like it when there’s fake team names. Chicago <i>Stars</i>? Ugh, so fake. It puts me in the mindset of, <i>Ugh, this makes everything feel so fake.</i> I dunno. I’m weird.<br /><br />Anyway, this book and I had a very rocky start. I didn’t like Phoebe. The story seemed like it was going to be stupid. And there were a couple writing issues that almost made me quit (there was a sentence comparing the players to plantation workers and their master that my body just physically rejected. And there was also that sentence about the lady who you knew was good with dogs because she had a <i>shiatsu</i>. Jesus.)<br /><br />Phoebe was really hard to take in the beginning (and sometimes in the middle and end as well), but the depth of her character surprised me, and I totally warmed up to her eventually. And while the story was a little ridiculous, it ended up being fun, not stupid :) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The only truly stupid thing was Dan forgoing a chip shot field goal on 4th down with 8 seconds left. STUPID man, you play for the tie in that situation! Grrr. Oh, and that stuff with Hardesty - that was super stupid, too :P  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Dan was a fricken caveman, but he could be kind of charming too. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And his glasses! I don’t know how or why, but the descriptions of him when he was wearing his glasses made him sound sooooo sexy ;)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />I ended up enjoying this overall. <b>3.5 stars</b> and rounding up, cuz I feel like this book "won me over" despite myself ;) This was the first time I've tried this author, and I wouldn't mind checking out some of her other stuff.<br /></span>

    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/720099328?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Ingie by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/7179798-susanne">Susanne </a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2014">books-i-read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-contemporary">romance-m-f-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=series-standalone-stories">series-standalone-stories</a>
